        var tabs = ["today","yesterday"];
        $(document).ready(function() {

            tabs.forEach(function(val) {
                $('#usa_table_countries_' + val).dataTable({

                    "scrollCollapse": true,
                    "scrollX": true,
                    "order": [

                        [2, 'desc']
                    ],
                    "sDom": '<"bottom"flp><"clear">',
                    "paging": false,

                    "initComplete": function(settings, json) {

                    },
                    columnDefs: [{
                            "searchable": false,
                            "orderable": false,
                            "targets": 0
                        },
                        {

                            orderSequence: ["asc", "desc"],
                            "targets": [1]
                        },
                        {

                            orderSequence: ["desc", "asc"],
                            "targets": "_all"
                        }
                    ],


                });

                $('#nav-' + val + '-tab a').click(function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    $(this).tab('show');
                })

                $('#usa_table_countries_' + val).on('order.dt search.dt', function() {

                    var $global_i = 1;
                    $('#usa_table_countries_' + val).DataTable().column(0, {
                        search: 'applied',
                        order: 'applied'
                    }).nodes().each(function(cell, i) {


                        if ($(cell).parent().hasClass("total_row_usa")) {

                            cell.innerHTML = '';
                        } else {
                            cell.innerHTML = $global_i;
                            $global_i++;
                        }

                        //console.log(cell);
                    });
                }).DataTable().draw();

              
                $('#usa_table_countries_today_filter input').on('change', function() {

                    $('#usa_table_countries_yesterday_filter input').val($(this).val());
                    $('#usa_table_countries_yesterday_filter input').keyup();

                })

                $('#usa_table_countries_yesterday_filter input').on('change', function() {

                    $('#usa_table_countries_today_filter input').val($(this).val());
                    $('#usa_table_countries_today_filter input').keyup();

                })


            });
        });

The announcement comes as the Department of Defense has awarded a&nbsp;contract&nbsp;for&nbsp;prefilled syringes for future COVID-19 vaccine: more than 100 million syringes&nbsp;for distribution across the United States by year-end 2020, with&nbsp;the &quot;ultimate production goal of <strong>over 500 million prefilled syringes</strong> (doses) <strong>in 2021</strong>.&quot; [<a href="https://www.defense.gov/Newsroom/Releases/Release/Article/2184808/dod-awards-138-million-contract-enabling-prefilled-syringes-for-future-covid-19/source/GovDelivery/" style="cursor: pointer;" target="_blank">source</a>]&nbsp;</li>
</ul>

</div></div><button style="margin-top:30px;" class="btn btn-light date-btn" data-date="2020-05-08">May 8&nbsp;&nbsp; <i class="fa fa-chevron-circle-down"></i></button><div class="newsdate_div" style="display: none;" id="newsdate2020-05-08"><span id="news" class="news_category_title">News</span><div class="news_post">
<div class="news_body news_box">
<ul>
<li>A 5-year-old died in New York City on Thursday from what appeared to be a rare syndrome linked to the coronavirus that causes life-threatening inflammation in children [<a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2020/05/06/health/kawasaki-disease-covid-coronavirus-children.html" style="cursor: pointer;" target="_blank">learn more</a>] [<a href="https://www.thelancet.com/journals/lancet/article/PIIS0140-6736(20)31094-1/fulltext" style="cursor: pointer;">study</a>], New York State Governor&nbsp;Andrew M. Cuomo said&nbsp;[<a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2020/05/08/nyregion/coronavirus-new-york-update.html#link-3a6c1cdb" style="cursor: pointer;" target="_blank">source</a>]<br />
<br />
This is at least the second death reported worldwide so far&nbsp;after that of a 14-year-old boy in England, according to a study published on May 7 in the journal Lancet [<a href="https://www.thelancet.com/journals/lancet/article/PIIS0140-6736(20)31094-1/fulltext" style="cursor: pointer;">source</a>].<br />
<br />
On April 27, the UK NHS had alerted about the new illness, with at least 12 children in the UK requiring intensive care, and an<strong>&nbsp;estimated &quot;4.5 cases for every 100,000 children under the age of 18 in the UK</strong>&quot; [<a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/apr/27/nhs-warns-of-rise-in-children-with-new-illness-that-may-be-linked-to-coronavirus" style="cursor: pointer;" target="_blank">source</a>]. One of the first reported cases of the illness in the US,&nbsp;a healthy 12-yea-old in Louisiana, almost died&nbsp;a few weeks ago [<a href="https://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-8276001/Healthy-12-year-old-girls-heart-stopped-developed-rare-heart-condition-linked-COVID-19.html" style="cursor: pointer;" target="_blank">source</a>]. Between&nbsp;&nbsp;April 17 and May 1, 15 children were hospitalized in New Yor City for the new&nbsp;illness [<a href="https://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-8288313/Fifteen-children-hospitalized-NYC-rare-deadly-Kawasaki-disease.html" style="cursor: pointer;" target="_blank">source</a>]</li>
</ul>

<script type="text/javascript">
            $(document).ready(function() {

                if ($('.news_post').length <= 0) {

                    $('#news').hide();

                }

                $(document).on('click', '.load-more__btn', function() {


                    var ID = $(this).attr('id');
                    var country = $(this).attr('data-country');
                    var region = $(this).attr('data-region');
                    var days_count = $(this).attr('data-days_count');


                    $('.load-more__btn').hide();
                    $('.loading').css('display', 'inline-block');
                    $.ajax({
                        type: 'POST',
                        url: '/coronavirus/news-block/news_main_updates.php',
                        data: 'fd=' + ID + (country ? '&country=' + country : '') + (region ? '&region=' + region : '') + (days_count ? '&days_count=' + days_count : ''),
                        success: function(html) {
                                $(ID).remove();
                                $('.loading').remove();
                                $('#news_block').append(html);


                                dateButtonsEvents();


                            }


                            ,
                        error: function(objAJAXRequest, strError) {
                            $('.loading').remove();
                            $('.load-more__btn').show();
                        }
                    });
                });
            });

            function dateButtonsEvents() {


                $('.date-btn').prop("onclick", null).off("click");
                $('.date-btn').on('click', function() {


                    var n = $('#newsdate' + $(this).data('date'));
                    if (n.is(':visible')) {
                        n.slideUp('fast');
                        $(this).find('i').removeClass('fa-chevron-circle-up');
                        $(this).find('i').addClass('fa-chevron-circle-down');
                    } else {
                        n.slideDown('fast');


                        $(this).find('i').removeClass('fa-chevron-circle-down');
                        $(this).find('i').addClass('fa-chevron-circle-up');
                    }
                });


            }
            $(document).ready(function() {



                dateButtonsEvents();
            });
        </script>

<h3>&nbsp;</h3>
<div id="innercontent">
<h2 id="pui">Patients Under Investigation (PUI) in the United States</h2>
<p>CDC in the early stages released information regarding the number of cases and people under investigation that was updated regularly on Mondays, Wednesdays, and Fridays. Below we provide the historical reports that we were able to gather in order to track the progression in the number of suspected cases and US states involved through time in the initial stages<br>
</p>

</table>
</div>
<h2 id="timeline">Timeline of Events</h2>
<div class="spaced">
<ul>
<li><img src="/img/alert.png" width="16" height="16"> <span class="style1"><a href="https://www.hhs.gov/about/news/2020/01/31/secretary-azar-declares-public-health-emergency-us-2019-novel-coronavirus.html">On January 31, HHS declared Coronavirus a Public Health Emergency in the US</a></span><br>
As of Jan. 31, the Wuhan coronavirus is officially a public health emergency in the United States, Alex Azar, secretary of the US Department of Health and Human Services (HHS), announced at a White House press briefing.</li>
<li><img src="/img/alert.png" width="16" height="16"> On Jan. 31, the U.S. Centers for Disease Control and Prevention (CDC) <strong>issued a federal quarantine for 14 days</strong> affecting the 195 American evacuees from Wuhan, China. Starting Sunday, Feb. 2, U.S. citizens, permanent residents and immediate family who have visited China's Hubei province will undergo a <strong>mandatory 14 days quarantine</strong> and, if they have visited other parts of China, they would be screened at airports and asked to self-quarantine for 14 days. The last time the CDC had issued a quarantine was over 50 years ago in the 1960s, for smallpox.</li>
<li><img src="/img/alert.png" width="16" height="16"> President Donald Trump signed an order on Jan. 31 for the U.S. to<strong> deny entry to foreign nationals who traveled to China</strong> within the preceding two weeks, aside from the immediate family of U.S. citizens.</li>
<li>On Jan. 30, the CDC had confirmed the<strong> first case of person to person transmission in the U.S.: </strong><strong><sup>[<a href="#ref-12">12</a>]</sup></strong> the husband of the Chicago, Illinois case who had returned from Wuhan, China on Jan. 13 and who tested positive for the virus on Jan. 24).</li>
<li>CDC stated on Jan. 30 that &quot;It is likely there will be more cases of 2019-nCoV reported in the U.S. in the coming days and weeks, including more person-to-person spread.&quot;<strong><sup>[<a href="#ref-12">12</a>]</sup></strong></li>
<li>The virus had been confirmed in <strong>5 states</strong>.</li>
<li>On Jan. 31, <strong> New York City</strong> health officials vehemently denied the rumor regarding a coronavirus case in the city .<strong><sup>[<a href="#ref-13">13</a>]</sup></strong>. On Feb. 1, however, the city's health commissioner did report that there was a test being performed on a person under 40 who had returned from China, developed matching symptoms, and tested negative to the seasonal flu.</li>
<li><strong>Most US patients had recently visited Wuhan</strong>.</li>
<li>All of the first five U.S. cases were described as <strong>mild</strong>.</li>
<li><a href="https://www.cnn.com/2020/01/31/health/washington-coronavirus-study-nejm/index.html?utm_term=link&utm_medium=social&utm_content=2020-02-01T00">A study on the first US case of novel coronavirus detailed mild symptoms followed by pneumonia</a></li>
</ul>
</div>
<h3>U.S. Airlines suspended ALL flights between the U.S. and China </h3>
<p>On Friday, January 31, Delta, American and United announced they would temporarily suspend all of their mainland China flights in response to the coronavirus outbreak.<strong><sup>[<a href="#ref-14">14</a>]</sup></strong></p>
<p> Prior to this January 31 announcement: </p>
<ul>
<li><strong>UNITED AIRLINES</strong><br>
on Jan. 28 had announced it would cut 24 flights between the U.S. and China for the first week of February.</li>
<li><strong>AMERICAN AIRLINES</strong><br>
on Jan. 29 had announced it would suspend flights from Los Angeles to Shanghai and Beijing from Feb. 9 through March 27, 2020. It will maintain its flight schedules (10 daily A/R) from Dallas-Fort Worth to Shanghai and Beijing, as well as from Los Angeles and Dallas-Fort Worth to Hong Kong.</li>
<li><strong>DELTA<br>
</strong> had not adjusted its schedule of direct flights from the U.S. to China. It is the only airline with direct flights to not take action so far. </li>
</ul>
The White House was considering issuing a ban on flights between the United States and China, as of late Jan. 28<strong><sup>[<a href="#ref-11">11</a>]</sup></strong>.
Italy has announced on January 31 that it was suspending all flights to and from China following the first 2 cases of coronavirus in Italy.
<h3>Travel Alert: Do Not Travel to China</h3>
<ul>
<li>The U.S. State Department on January 30 issued a <strong><a href="https://travel.state.gov/content/travel/en/traveladvisories/traveladvisories/china-travel-advisory.html">Level 4: Do Not Travel to China Alert</a></strong> <strong><sup>[<a href="#ref-4">4</a>]</sup></strong> (the highest level of alert). </li>
<li>Previously, on January 29, the advisory was set at a lower &quot;Level 3: Reconsider Travel&quot; advising not to travel to Hubei Province: (Level 4) and reconsider travel to the remainder of China (Level 3).</li>
<li>The CDC on Jan. 28 issued a <a href="https://wwwnc.cdc.gov/travel/notices/warning/novel-coronavirus-china">Level 3 Warning</a>, recommending that travelers <strong>avoid all nonessential travel to China </strong><sup></sup><strong><sup>[<a href="#ref-5">5</a>]</sup></strong>.<br>
</li>
</ul>
<h4>Screening incoming passengers at 20 airports in the U.S. </h4>
<p>On January 17, the CDC announced that 3 airports in the United States would begin screening incoming passengers from China: SFO, JFK, and LAX <strong><sup>[<a href="#ref-6">6</a>]</sup></strong> Other 2 airports were added subsequently, and on January 28, the U.S. Department of Health and Human Services (HHS) announced that 15 additional U.S. airports (bringing the total to 20) would begin screening incoming travelers from China. </p>
<p>Below is the complete list of airports where screening for the 2019 Novel Coronavirus (2019-nCoV) is in place: </p>
<ul><li>Los Angeles International (LAX) </li>
<li>San Francisco International (SFO) </li>
<li>Chicago O'Hare</li>
<li>New York JFK</li>
<li>Atlanta Hartsfield-Jackson International</li>
<li>Houston George Bush Intercontinental </li>
<li>Dallas-Fort Worth International</li>
<li>San Diego International</li>
<li>Seattle-Tacoma International</li>
<li>Honolulu International</li>
<li>Anchorage Ted Stevens International</li>
<li>Minneapolis-St. Paul International</li>
<li>Detroit Metropolitan</li>
<li>Miami International</li>
<li>Washington Dulles International</li>
<li>Philadelphia International</li>
<li>Newark Liberty International</li>
<li>Boston Logan International</li>
<li>El Paso International</li>
<li>Puerto Rico's San Juan Airport</li>
</ul>

<script>
/*    var states_list = [];
    var states_items = [];*/
    $(document).ready(function() {

        if (window.location.href.indexOf('#contactModalForm') != -1) {
            $('#contactModalForm').modal('show');
        }

        //var states_items = states_list.map(function(x) { return { item: x }; });

        $('#states_select').selectize({
            persist: false,
            labelField: 'entity_name',
            valueField: 'cca3',
            searchField: [
                'cca3', 'entity_name'
            ],
            options: states_items,
            onChange: function(value, isOnInitialize) {

                
                if (states_list[value] && states_list[value]['counties']) {

                    // show counties                    
                    var counties = states_list[value]['counties'];

                    if ($('#counties_select')[0].selectize) {

                        $('#counties_select')[0].selectize.destroy();
                    }

                    $('#counties_select').selectize({
                        persist: false,
                        labelField: 'name',
                        valueField: 'name',
                        searchField: [
                            'name'
                        ],
                        options: counties,
                    });

                } else {


                    // remove counties
                    if ($('#counties_select')[0].selectize) {



                        $('#counties_select')[0].selectize.destroy();


                    }
                    $('#counties_select').hide();
                    $('#counties_select').find('options').remove();

                }
            }

        });



        $("a[href='/contact/']").after('| <a href="/report_us/">report coronavirus cases</a>');

        $("a[href='/report_us/']").on('click', function() {


            $('#contactModalForm').modal('show');


            return false;
        });


    });
</script>

<script>
    function validateEmail(email) {
        var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(email);
    }

    function scrollIntoViewIfNeeded(target) {
        var rect = target.getBoundingClientRect();
        if (rect.bottom > window.innerHeight) {
            target.scrollIntoView(false);
        }
        if (rect.top < 0) {
            target.scrollIntoView();
        }
    }

    function showErrorMessage(msg) {
        scrollIntoViewIfNeeded($(".statusMsg")[0]);
        $('.statusMsg').html('<span style="color:red;">' + msg + '</span>').fadeOut(200).fadeIn(200);
    }

    function showConfirmForm(e) {

        var form = $('#contactForm');

        var all_empty = true;

        if (form.find('#states_select option:selected').text() != '') {


            all_empty = false;
            $('#confirm_state').html('<strong>USA state/territory: </strong>' + form.find('#states_select option:selected').text());
        } else {

            showErrorMessage('"State" field is required');
            return false;
            $('#confirm_state').html('');
        }

        Object.keys(reports_types).forEach(function(report_type) {

            var report_type_label = reports_types[report_type];

            if (form.find('#new_' + report_type).val() != '') {
                all_empty = false;
                $('#confirm_new_' + report_type).html('<strong>New ' + report_type_label +
                    ': </strong>' + form.find('#new_' + report_type).val());
            } else {
                $('#confirm_new_' + report_type).html('');
            }

            if (form.find('#total_' + report_type).val() != '') {
                all_empty = false;
                $('#confirm_total_' + report_type).html('<strong>Total ' + report_type_label +
                    ': </strong>' + form.find('#total_' + report_type).val());
            } else {
                $('#confirm_total_' + report_type).html('');
            }

        });

        if (form.find('#counties_select option:selected').text() != '') {

            all_empty = false;
            $('#confirm_county').html('<strong>USA county: </strong>' + form.find('#counties_select option:selected').text());

        } else {


            $('#confirm_county').html('');
        }
        if (form.find('#email').val() != '') {

            if (!validateEmail(form.find('#email').val())) {

                showErrorMessage('Bad email address format, please fix');
                return false;

            }

            all_empty = false;
            $('#confirm_email').html('<strong>Email: </strong>' + form.find('#email').val());
        } else {
            $('#confirm_email').html('');
        }

        if (form.find('#url').val() != '') {
            all_empty = false;

            $('#confirm_url').html('<strong>URL: </strong>' + form.find('#url').val());
        } else {
            showErrorMessage('"Source URL" field is required');
            return false;

            $('#confirm_url').html('');
        }

        if (form.find('#message').val() != '') {
            all_empty = false;
            $('#confirm_message').html('<strong>Comment: </strong>' + form.find('#message').val());
        } else {
            $('#confirm_message').html('');
        }


        e.preventDefault();
        $('#contactModalForm').modal('hide');
        $('.statusMsg').html('');
        $('#contactModalFormConfirm').modal('show');


    }

    function backToContactForm(e) {

        e.preventDefault();
        $('#contactModalFormConfirm').modal('hide');
        $('#contactModalForm').modal('show');

    }

    // clear contact form values
    function resetContactForm() {

        //$('#contactForm')[0].reset();
        $(':input', '#contactForm')
            .not(':button', ':submit', ':reset', ':hidden', '#email')
            .val('')
            .prop('checked', false)
            .prop('selected', false);

        if ($('#states_select')[0] && $('#states_select')[0].selectize) {

            $("#states_select")[0].selectize.clear();
        }

        if ($('#counties_select')[0] && $('#counties_select')[0].selectize) {
            $("#counties_select")[0].selectize.clear();
        }
        $(".statusMsg").html('');

    }

    function submitContactForm(e) {
        var re = /^[0-9]*$/i;
        /*  var new_cases = $('#new_cases').val();
          var total_cases = $('#total_cases').val();



          if (!re.test(new_cases)) {
              alert('New cases should have numbers only.');
              new_cases.focus();
              return false;
          } else if (!re.test(total_cases)) {
              alert('Total cases should have numbers only.');
              total_cases.focus();
              return false;
          }*/

        e.preventDefault();

        var form = $('#contactForm');
        var url = form.attr('action');

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: url,
            data: form.serialize(),
            success: function(data) {


                $('#contactModalFormConfirm').modal('hide');

                resetContactForm();

                alert('Thank you');
                window.location.reload(false);

            }
        });



    }
</script>
<h2>Countries:</h2>
<div class="spaced" style="margin-top:20px ">
